Documentation Obligations

Non-code compliance items required by the standard. These do not fail the gate but must be addressed for full regulatory compliance.

Rule Clause Obligation Guidance
IEC62304-5.1.15.1.1software-development-plan: A Software Development Plan must be established and maintainedCreate and maintain a Software Development Plan covering lifecycle activities, deliverables, and traceability
IEC62304-5.1.65.1.6software-verification-plan: A Software Verification Plan must define verification activities and acceptance criteriaDocument verification strategy including unit tests, integration tests, and acceptance criteria
IEC62304-5.2.15.2.1software-requirements-specification: Software requirements must be documented and traceable to system requirementsCreate a Software Requirements Specification (SRS) with traceable requirements
IEC62304-5.3.15.3.1architecture-documentation: Software architecture must be documented showing subdivision into software itemsDocument software architecture with component diagrams and interface descriptions
IEC62304-5.4.15.4.1detailed-design: Detailed design documentation is required for Class C software itemsCreate detailed design documents for each software unit including algorithms and data structures
IEC62304-6.16.1maintenance-plan: A Software Maintenance Plan must be establishedEstablish a maintenance plan covering feedback handling, modification analysis, and release procedures
IEC62304-7.1.17.1.1risk-analysis: Software risk analysis per ISO 14971 must be performed and documentedPerform and document risk analysis in accordance with ISO 14971, including hazard identification and risk control
IEC62304-8.1.18.1.1configuration-management: A Configuration Management system must be established for all software itemsImplement configuration management covering version control, change control, and baseline identification
